```r
df <- tibble(x = c(1, NA, 3))
filter(df, x > 1)
```

```
## # A tibble: 1 × 1
##       x
##   <dbl>
## 1     3
```

```r
filter(df, is.na(x) | x > 1)
```

```
## # A tibble: 2 × 1
##       x
##   <dbl>
## 1    NA
## 2     3
```

```r
select(flights, starts_with("dep"), starts_with("arr"))
```

```
## # A tibble: 336,776 × 4
##    dep_time dep_delay arr_time arr_delay
```
